\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01200}01200     \textcolor{comment}{// THIS IS ON PURPOSE AND BY DESIGN.  The background color feature}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01201}01201     \textcolor{comment}{// has typically been used with the 'classic' font to overwrite old}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01202}01202     \textcolor{comment}{// screen contents with new data.  This ONLY works because the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01203}01203     \textcolor{comment}{// characters are a uniform size; it's not a sensible thing to do with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01204}01204     \textcolor{comment}{// proportionally-\/spaced fonts with glyphs of varying sizes (and that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01205}01205     \textcolor{comment}{// may overlap).  To replace previously-\/drawn text when using a custom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01206}01206     \textcolor{comment}{// font, use the getTextBounds() function to determine the smallest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01207}01207     \textcolor{comment}{// rectangle encompassing a string, erase the area with fillRect(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01208}01208     \textcolor{comment}{// then draw new text.  This WILL infortunately 'blink' the text, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01209}01209     \textcolor{comment}{// is unavoidable.  Drawing 'background' pixels will NOT fix this,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01210}01210     \textcolor{comment}{// only creates a new set of problems.  Have an idea to work around}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01211}01211     \textcolor{comment}{// this (a canvas object type for MCUs that can afford the RAM and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01212}01212     \textcolor{comment}{// displays supporting setAddrWindow() and pushColors()), but haven't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{batt___adafruit___g_f_x_8cpp_source_l01213}01213     \textcolor{comment}{// implemented this yet.}}
